<h4><span id=".E5.9C.BA.E5.9C.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="场地">场地</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="编辑章节：场地">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1440" data-file-width="2560" decoding="async" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg/220px-Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg/330px-Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg/440px-Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Belgrad_Nikola_Tesla_airport.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E6%A0%BC%E8%8E%B1%E5%BE%B7%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E6%9C%BA%E5%9C%BA" title="贝尔格莱德尼古拉·特斯拉机场">贝尔格莱德尼古拉·特斯拉机场</a>于2006年以这位科学家的名字命名</div></div></div>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Nikola Tesla Memorial Center" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尼古拉·特斯拉纪念中心"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E7%BA%AA%E5%BF%B5%E4%B8%AD%E5%BF%83&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尼古拉·特斯拉纪念中心（页面不存在）">尼古拉·特斯拉纪念中心</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikola_Tesla_Memorial_Center" title="en:Nikola Tesla Memorial Center"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Nikola Tesla Memorial Center</span></a></span>）</span></span>，位于<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E7%BD%97%E5%9C%B0%E4%BA%9A" title="克罗地亚">克罗地亚</a>斯米尔扬</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E6%A0%BC%E8%8E%B1%E5%BE%B7%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E6%9C%BA%E5%9C%BA" title="贝尔格莱德尼古拉·特斯拉机场">贝尔格莱德尼古拉·特斯拉机场</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-318"><a href="#cite_note-318">[311]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%A6%86" title="尼古拉·特斯拉博物馆">尼古拉·特斯拉博物馆</a>，位于<a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E6%A0%BC%E8%8E%B1%E5%BE%B7" title="贝尔格莱德">贝尔格莱德</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-319"><a href="#cite_note-319">[312]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-320"><a href="#cite_note-320">[313]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%80%E8%A1%93%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%A4%A8_(%E8%96%A9%E6%A0%BC%E5%8B%92%E5%B8%83)" title="技術博物館 (薩格勒布)">尼古拉·特斯拉技术博物馆</a>，位于克罗地亚<a href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E6%A0%BC%E5%8B%92%E5%B8%83" title="萨格勒布">萨格勒布</a>，于2015年以这位科学家的名字命名</li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="TPP Nikola Tesla" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尼古拉·特斯拉发电厂"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%8F%91%E7%94%B5%E5%8E%82&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尼古拉·特斯拉发电厂（页面不存在）">尼古拉·特斯拉发电厂</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TPP_Nikola_Tesla" title="en:TPP Nikola Tesla"><span dir="auto" lang="en">TPP Nikola Tesla</span></a></span>）</span></span>，位于塞尔维亚，是当地最大的发电厂，于1970年首次投产</li>
<li>截至2008年11月，克罗地亚有128条街道以尼古拉·特斯拉的名字命名，使他成为该国第八个最常见的街道名称来源<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-321"><a href="#cite_note-321">[314]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E9%99%A8%E7%9F%B3%E5%9D%91" title="特斯拉陨石坑">特斯拉陨石坑</a>，月球远端的一个26公里宽的火山口<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Minorplanet_322-0"><a href="#cite_note-Minorplanet-322">[315]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E8%A1%8C%E6%98%9F2244" title="小行星2244">2244 特斯拉</a>，一颗小行星<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Minorplanet_322-1"><a href="#cite_note-Minorplanet-322">[315]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E5.AD.A6.E6.A0.A1"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="学校">学校</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="编辑章节：学校">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tesla STEM High School" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="特斯拉STEM高中"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89STEM%E9%AB%98%E4%B8%AD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="特斯拉STEM高中（页面不存在）">特斯拉STEM高中</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tesla_STEM_High_School" title="en:Tesla STEM High School"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Tesla STEM High School</span></a></span>）</span></span>于2012年在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8E%E7%9B%9B%E9%A1%BF%E5%B7%9E" title="华盛顿州">华盛顿州</a><a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B7%E5%BE%B7%E8%92%99%E5%BE%B7_(%E5%8D%8E%E7%9B%9B%E9%A1%BF%E5%B7%9E)" title="雷德蒙德 (华盛顿州)">雷德蒙市</a>创建，是一所专注于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Science, technology, engineering, and mathematics" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="科学、技术、工程和数学"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E3%80%81%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E3%80%81%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%92%8C%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="科学、技术、工程和数学（页面不存在）">科学、技术、工程和数学</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science,_technology,_engineering,_and_mathematics" title="en:Science, technology, engineering, and mathematics"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Science, technology, engineering, and mathematics</span></a></span>）</span></span>学科的<span class="rt-commentedText" style="display: inline-block; border-bottom: 1px dotted;" title="choice school">选择学校</span>。这个名字是由学生投票决定的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-323"><a href="#cite_note-323">[316]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E8.88.B9.E8.88.B6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="船舶">船舶</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="编辑章节：船舶">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>SS Nikola Tesla，一艘<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E8%BD%AE" title="自由轮">自由轮</a>，1943年8月31日铺设，1943年9月25日下水，1947年从政府服务中出售，1970年报废</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.E6.9C.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="计算机">计算机</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="编辑章节：计算机">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tesla (microarchitecture)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="特斯拉 (微架构)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89_(%E5%BE%AE%E6%9E%B6%E6%9E%84)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="特斯拉 (微架构)（页面不存在）">特斯拉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tesla_(microarchitecture)" title="en:Tesla (microarchitecture)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Tesla (microarchitecture)</span></a></span>）</span></span>，<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E4%BC%9F%E8%BE%BE" title="英伟达">英伟达</a>公司开发的一种显卡图形处理单元微架构</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E8.B4.A7.E5.B8.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="货币">货币</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="编辑章节：货币">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%A4%AB%E7%AC%AC%E7%BA%B3%E5%B0%94" title="南斯拉夫第纳尔">南斯拉夫第纳尔</a>1970年（雕像）和1993年之间的6种不同的纸币上印有特斯拉</li>
<li>100<a href="/wiki/%E5%A1%9E%E7%88%BE%E7%B6%AD%E4%BA%9E%E7%AC%AC%E7%B4%8D%E7%88%BE" title="塞爾維亞第納爾">塞尔维亚第纳尔</a>的纸币上印有特斯拉</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E6.B8.B8.E6.88.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="游戏">游戏</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="编辑章节：游戏">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A2%E8%89%B2%E8%AD%A6%E6%88%92%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%97" title="红色警戒系列">红色警戒</a>》中，有以他名字命名的武器“特斯拉线圈”，也被译为“磁暴线圈”</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%BA%E5%AE%A2%E6%95%99%E6%A2%9D%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%97" title="刺客教條系列">刺客信条</a>2》中的“真相”指出，特斯拉拥有能给人类带来先进科技的4号金苹果，并计划让世界有用之不尽的能源，特斯拉因此成为圣殿骑士们（爱迪生等人）攻击的对象</li>
<li>線上遊戲《王者之劍》中，副本「混沌之塔」有以他名字命名的怪物“特斯拉線圈”，以釋放強力電擊攻擊玩家</li>
<li>遊戲《<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%8B%E5%9B%BD%E4%BF%9D%E5%8D%AB%E6%88%98%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%97" title="王国保卫战系列">王国保卫战系列</a>》中，由矮人工程師所製造以釋放電擊來攻擊敵人的塔被命名為“特斯拉X104 (TESLA X104)”</li>
<li>遊戲《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="MouseHunt" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="MouseHunt"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=MouseHunt&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="MouseHunt（页面不存在）">MouseHunt</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MouseHunt" title="en:MouseHunt"><span dir="auto" lang="en">MouseHunt</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中，一款限量版的捕鼠陷阱被稱為“Chesla Revenge”。Chesla意指Cheese（乳酪）與Tesla（特斯拉）。它釋放強大的電力來攻擊老鼠</li>
<li>遊戲《<a href="/wiki/%E7%B5%95%E5%9C%B0%E8%A6%81%E5%A1%9E2" title="絕地要塞2">絕地要塞2</a>》的官方數位漫畫中提及，特斯拉為1850年代的藍組工程師，並使用一袋藍圖以建造輔助建築物</li>
<li>手機遊戲《<a href="/wiki/%E9%83%A8%E8%90%BD%E5%86%B2%E7%AA%81" title="部落冲突">部落冲突</a>》、《皇室戰爭》中，有以他名字命名的建築設備“特斯拉電磁塔”</li>
<li>遊戲《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Order:_1886" title="The Order: 1886">The Order: 1886</a>》中，提供主角的團隊各種武器</li>
<li>手機遊戲《勇者的盆栽》Heroes Flick中，有以他和摩根的故事作藍本的角色 - 科研之子達士拿</li>
<li>手機遊戲《<a href="/wiki/Fate/Grand_Order" title="Fate/Grand Order">Fate/Grand Order</a>》中，以「Archer」的職階登場，拥有EX寶具「人類神話‧雷電降臨」</li>
<li>遊戲《<a href="/wiki/%E9%AC%A5%E9%99%A3%E7%89%B9%E6%94%BB" title="鬥陣特攻">鬥陣特攻</a>》中，猩猩科学家「Winston」所使用的武器电机枪被命名为「特斯拉电磁炮」</li>
<li>遊戲《robocraft》中，創建機械人的裝備選項有「特斯拉刀」</li>
<li>遊戲《They are billions》中有功能為無線輸電的「特斯拉塔」</li>
<li>手機遊戲《<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A2%E7%95%8C%E7%89%A9%E8%AA%9E" title="夢界物語">夢界物語</a>》中其中一位導靈</li>
<li>手機遊戲《造物法則》中主角夜北的載體(主角夜北的前載體為愛迪生，後為特斯拉)</li>
<li>手機遊戲《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B4%A9%E5%A3%9E3rd" title="崩壞3rd">崩壞3rd</a>》中的登場角色及聖痕，改編自現實的特斯拉</li>
<li>遊戲《碧血狂殺 2》中，有他的支線故事&lt;聰明的天才男孩&gt;，在1898年，特斯拉曾展示可遠端操控的船模通過無線電波來操作螺旋槳和燈光，當時船模配有多塊大號電池以及無線電信號控制器遠端控制 (或遠端自動化) 的理念至今也被人們廣為應用</li>
<li>手機遊戲《CODE:SEED 星火之歌》中的一名攻擊型遊戲角色，特斯拉 模組為3D角色並攻擊招式都為電系招式</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E5.BD.B1.E8.A6.96.E4.BD.9C.E5.93.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="影視作品">影視作品</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="编辑章节：影視作品">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>2006年電影《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%B4%E5%91%BD%E9%AD%94%E6%9C%AF" title="致命魔术">致命魔术</a>》提到特斯拉，片中他發明的放大發射器能夠多次複製各種物體（包括生命體）</li>
<li>2008年電影《<a href="/wiki/K20%EF%BC%9A%E6%80%AA%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E9%9D%A2%E7%9B%B8" title="K20：怪人二十面相">K20：怪人二十面相</a>》中虚构出特斯拉的“特斯拉装置”。该装置可以使电器不借助电线便运行起来，比如在数米之外运行特斯拉装置，可以使一颗没有放入台灯中的台灯灯泡发光</li>
<li>2008年電視劇《<a href="/wiki/%E7%95%B0%E5%BD%A2%E5%BA%87%E8%AD%B7%E6%89%80" title="異形庇護所">異形庇護所</a>》中，他被描述為擁有血族的天才科學家，由於注射遠古血族的血液而覺醒為世界上最後一個血族（特裔）</li>
<li>2015年電影《<a href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E6%97%A5%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C_(%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1)" title="明日世界 (电影)">明日世界</a>》將特斯拉與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E8%BF%AA%E7%94%9F" title="愛迪生">愛迪生</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E8%8F%B2%E7%88%BE" title="艾菲爾">艾菲爾</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%A1%E5%B0%94%E7%BA%B3" title="凡尔纳">凡爾纳</a>視為明日世界的創造者</li>
<li>2019年電影《<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%B5%81%E5%A4%A7%E6%88%B0_(%E9%9B%BB%E5%BD%B1)" title="電流大戰 (電影)">電流大戰</a>》描述<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%94%E6%B2%BB%C2%B7%E5%A8%81%E6%96%AF%E6%B1%80%E8%B1%AA%E6%96%AF" title="乔治·威斯汀豪斯">喬治·威斯汀豪斯</a>與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E8%BF%AA%E7%94%9F" title="愛迪生">愛迪生</a>為爭取美國最大供電商的稱號所引發的商業競爭</li>
<li>2020年電影《<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89_(2020%E5%B9%B4%E9%9B%BB%E5%BD%B1)" title="特斯拉 (2020年電影)">特斯拉</a>》描述特斯拉的生平故事，包括交流電的發明以及與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E8%BF%AA%E7%94%9F" title="愛迪生">愛迪生</a>的激烈對抗</li>
<li>2020年電視劇《<a href="/wiki/%E7%95%B0%E4%B8%96%E5%A5%87%E4%BA%BA_(%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%9712)" title="異世奇人 (系列12)">神秘博士</a>》第十二季第四集《尼古拉·特斯拉驚魂夜》中，特斯拉偶然發現一外星記錄儀並對其回複信息，信息被另一外星種族截獲，後者的女王以地球生命安危要挾特斯拉為其修理損壞的太空飛船</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E6.BC.AB.E7.95.AB.E4.BD.9C.E5.93.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="漫畫作品">漫畫作品</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="编辑章节：漫畫作品">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>漫畫《造物法則》中作為主角的載體登場</li>
<li>漫畫《<a href="/wiki/%E7%B5%82%E6%9C%AB%E7%9A%84%E5%A5%B3%E6%AD%A6%E7%A5%9E" title="終末的女武神">終末的女武神</a>》中作為人類參戰方之一的鬥士</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.A6.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參見">參見</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="编辑章节：參見">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tesla Electric Light and Manufacturing" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="特斯拉電燈與製造公司"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E9%9B%BB%E7%87%88%E8%88%87%E8%A3%BD%E9%80%A0%E5%85%AC%E5%8F%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="特斯拉電燈與製造公司（页面不存在）">特斯拉電燈與製造公司</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tesla_Electric_Light_and_Manufacturing" title="en:Tesla Electric Light and Manufacturing"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Tesla Electric Light and Manufacturing</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="List of things named after Nikola Tesla" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="以尼古拉·特斯拉命名的事物清单"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%A5%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%91%BD%E5%90%8D%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%8D%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="以尼古拉·特斯拉命名的事物清单（页面不存在）">以尼古拉·特斯拉命名的事物清单</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_things_named_after_Nikola_Tesla" title="en:List of things named after Nikola Tesla"><span dir="auto" lang="en">List of things named after Nikola Tesla</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Nikola Tesla in popular culture" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="大众文化中的尼古拉·特斯拉"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E4%BC%97%E6%96%87%E5%8C%96%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="大众文化中的尼古拉·特斯拉（页面不存在）">大众文化中的尼古拉·特斯拉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikola_Tesla_in_popular_culture" title="en:Nikola Tesla in popular culture"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Nikola Tesla in popular culture</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%A5%E7%88%BE%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%99%AE%E7%BE%85%E9%80%8F%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%96%AF%E6%B3%B0%E5%9B%A0%E6%A2%85%E8%8C%A8" title="查爾斯·普羅透斯·斯泰因梅茨">查尔斯·普罗透斯·斯泰因梅茨</a>——同时代的交流电和高电压研究的电气先锋</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E9%AB%98%C2%B7%E6%B3%95%E6%8B%89%E7%AC%AC" title="米高·法拉第">迈克尔·法拉第</a></li></ul>

<h2><span id=".E6.B3.A8.E9.87.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="编辑章节：注释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="notelist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-31">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">特斯拉没有提到这是哪位教授的名字，但一些资料认为这是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Martin Sekulić" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="马丁·塞库利奇"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A9%AC%E4%B8%81%C2%B7%E5%A1%9E%E5%BA%93%E5%88%A9%E5%A5%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="马丁·塞库利奇（页面不存在）">马丁·塞库利奇</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martin_Sekuli%C4%87" title="en:Martin Sekulić"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Martin Sekulić</span></a></span>）</span></span>教授。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-131"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-131">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：Within the room were suspended two hard-rubber plates covered with tin foil. These were about fifteen feet apart and served as terminals of the wires leading from the transformers. When the current was turned on, the lamps or tubes, which had no wires connected to them, but lay on a table between the suspended plates, or which might be held in the hand in almost any part of the room, were made luminous. These were the same experiments and the same apparatus shown by Tesla in London about two years previous, "where they produced so much wonder and astonishment".</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-213"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-213">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：I have been feeding pigeons, thousands of them for years. But there was one, a beautiful bird, pure white with light grey tips on its wings; that one was different. It was a female. I had only to wish and call her and she would come flying to me. I loved that pigeon as a man loves a woman, and she loved me. As long as I had her, there was a purpose to my life.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-236"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-236">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：His [Tesla's] thoughts and efforts during at least the past 15 years were primarily of a speculative, philosophical, and somewhat promotional character often concerned with the production and wireless transmission of power; but did not include new, sound, workable principles or methods for realizing such results.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-264"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-264">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：He had no hobby, cared for no sort of amusement of any kind and lived in utter disregard of the most elementary rules of hygiene ... His method was inefficient in the extreme, for an immense ground had to be covered to get anything at all unless blind chance intervened and, at first, I was almost a sorry witness of his doings, knowing that just a little theory and calculation would have saved him 90 percent of the labor. But he had a veritable contempt for book learning and mathematical knowledge, trusting himself entirely to his inventor's instinct and practical American sense.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-275"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-275">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：I hold that space cannot be curved, for the simple reason that it can have no properties. It might as well be said that God has properties. He has not, but only attributes and these are of our own making. Of properties we can only speak when dealing with matter filling the space. To say that in the presence of large bodies space becomes curved is equivalent to stating that something can act upon nothing. I, for one, refuse to subscribe to such a view.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-281"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-281">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：... man's new sense of pity began to interfere with the ruthless workings of nature. The only method compatible with our notions of civilization and the race is to prevent the breeding of the unfit by sterilization and the deliberate guidance of the mating instinct ... The trend of opinion among eugenists is that we must make marriage more difficult. Certainly no one who is not a desirable parent should be permitted to produce progeny. A century from now it will no more occur to a normal person to mate with a person eugenically unfit than to marry a habitual criminal.</span>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
